Usage: 
  addSuperOrg.sh up|down|generate [-c <channel name>] [-t <timeout>] [-d <delay>] [-f <docker-compose-file>] [-s <dbtype>]
  addSuperOrg.sh -h|--help (print this message)
    <mode> - one of 'up', 'down', or 'generate'
      - 'up' - add superOrg to the sample network. You need to bring up the test network and create a channel first.
      - 'down' - bring down the test network and superOrg nodes
      - 'generate' - generate required certificates and org definition
    -c <channel name> - test network channel name (defaults to "mychannel")
    -ca <use CA> -  Use a CA to generate the crypto material
    -t <timeout> - CLI timeout duration in seconds (defaults to 10)
    -d <delay> - delay duration in seconds (defaults to 3)
    -s <dbtype> - the database backend to use: goleveldb (default) or couchdb
    -verbose - verbose mode

Typically, one would first generate the required certificates and 
genesis block, then bring up the network. e.g.:

	addSuperOrg.sh generate
	addSuperOrg.sh up
	addSuperOrg.sh up -c mychannel -s couchdb
	addSuperOrg.sh down

Taking all defaults:
	addSuperOrg.sh up
	addSuperOrg.sh down
